dadebulia mxolod mosaCveneblad, im ganzraxvis


 gareSe, rom mas iuridiuli Sedegi mohyves. 


zemoT miTiTebuli garemoebani ar adasture


ben im faqts, rom mxareebs ar surdaT 


garigebidan gamomdinare iuridiuli Sedegis da


dgoma. aRniSnulis dadasturebis tvirTi 


ekuTvnis d. k-Zes. mis mier miTiTebuli garemo


ebani ki aseTi saxis garigebis arsebobas ver 


adasturebs. m. C-Zis ganmartebebidan ki ir


kveva, rom mas swored aRniSnul farTze 


sakuTrebis uflebis mopoveba surda, radgan

uZravi qonebis SeZeniT SeiZleba dadges. is 


faqti, rom TiTqos m. C-Zes mosarCelisaTvis Se

xelSekrulebiT gansazRvruli valdebulebis

ruleba iZulebiT iqna dadebuli palata ver

iwvevs iseTi iZuleba, romelsac Tavisi xa

remoebad, romelic d. k-Zes afiqrebinebda, rom

i iZulebis ganmapirobebeli faqti unda

ebebs, romelic mxares afiqrebinebs, rom

ul safrTxeSi Caagdebs. aseT SemTxvevaSi 


ganqorwinebis muqara ar SeiZleba iyos iseTi

adamiani aiZulos yvelaferi gayidos rac abadia

nawilis mixedviT, saapelacio sasamarTlos mier damtkicebulad cnobili faqtobrivi

saTvis, Tu wamoyenebuli


 ar aris dasaSvebi 


da dasabuTebuli sakasacio pretenzia. dasaSveb da dasabuTebul sakasacio pretenziaSi 


igulisxmeba miTiTeba im procesualur darRvev


ebze, romlebic daSvebuli iyo saapelacio

Sefaseba.

cnobili, rom v. R-Ze sadavo saxlis mesakuTre ar aris. 


aRniSnuli faqtobrivi garemoebis mimarT kasatoris mier ar aris warmodgenili dasaSvebi da 


dasabuTebuli sakasacio pretenzia. kasatori ver miuTiTebs saqmeSi arsebul iseT 


mtkicebulebaze, romelic ar Seafasa sa


apelacio sasamarTlom da, romliTac 


dadasturdeboda v. R-Zis sakuTrebis ufleba


 sadavo saxlze. Sesabamisad, sakasacio 


sasamarTlo ar iziarebs kasatoris mosazreb

mesakuTrea.

sasamarTlos gadawyvetileba dausabuTebelia da


 Tvlis, rom saapelacio sasamarTlom swori 


samarTlebrivi Sefaseba misca dadgenil faqtobriv garemoebebs.

 sasamarTlom marTebulad ar daakmayofila

cio saCivari ar efuZneba imas, rom gadawyvetileba kanonis 


darRveviTaa gamotanili.

kicebulebebs sakasacio sasamarTlo sakasacio saCivris
